==========================The_first_checker_query=========================
You are an expert in writing java rule checkers and I need your help to generate a custom java rule checker in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
I will give you a rule description, which may contain multiple violations. You just need to generate a checker that can check the violations of the given test case.

The following is a description of the rule and the corresponding counterexample test case and the AST of the counterexample test case:

Rule description: Reports classes that may be made final because they cannot be extended from outside their compilation unit anyway. This is because all their constructors are private, so a subclass could not call the super constructor.;
The test case corresponding to the rule:
```
// Simple violation
public class Foo {
    private Foo() { }
}
The description of this test case is: bad 1
The number of violating the rule in this test case is: 1

```

  ——ASTModifierList
  ——ASTClassOrInterfaceBody
    ——ASTConstructorDeclaration
      ——ASTModifierList
      ——ASTFormalParameters (size = 0)
      ——ASTBlock

Note, when there are consecutive method calls, the last call is at the upper level of the syntax tree.


==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (node.isPublic() && !node.isFinal()) {
            NodeStream<ASTConstructorDeclaration> constructors = node.getDeclaredType().getConstructors();
            if (constructors.noneMatch(constructor -> !constructor.isPrivate())) {
                addViolation(data, node);
```java
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

==========5轮中每一轮为第一个测试用例生成的checker===============
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

=========================error_testcase_logics=========================
1. Get the name of the class.
2. Check whether the class is public.
3. Get all constructors of the class.
4. Check whether all constructors are private.
5. Check whether the class has any inner classes.
6. For each inner class, check whether it extends the outer class.
7. Check whether the inner class is public and static.
8. Check whether the inner class has a constructor that calls the super constructor.

If all constructors of the class are private, and there are no inner classes extending the class (except for public static inner classes that call the super constructor), then the class may be made final because it cannot be extended from outside its compilation unit. In this test case, the class `Foo` has a private constructor, but it has a public static inner class `Bar` that extends `Foo` and calls the super constructor, so the rule is not violated. The number of violations is 0.

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean hasNestedSubclass = node.descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration::isNested)
                    .anyMatch(nested -> nested.getSuperClassTypeNode() != null && nested.getSuperClassTypeNode().getType().getSymbol().equals(node.getSymbol()));
                if (!hasNestedSubclass) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean hasSubclassInSameUnit = node.descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(n -> n.getSuperClassTypeNode() != null && n.getSuperClassTypeNode().getType() != null)
                    .anyMatch(n -> n.getSuperClassTypeNode().getType().getSymbol().equals(node.getTypeMirror().getSymbol()));
                if (!hasSubclassInSameUnit) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
import java.lang.*;
```

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean hasNestedSubclass = node.descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration::isNested)

                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

        return super.visit(node, data);

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean hasSubclassInSameCompilationUnit = node.descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration::isNested)
                    .anyMatch(nested -> nested.getExtendsList().stream()
                        .anyMatch(extend -> extend.getType() != null && extend.getType().getSymbol().equals(node.getSymbol())));
                if (!hasSubclassInSameCompilationUnit) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

Rule description: Reports classes that may be made final because they cannot be extended from outside their compilation unit anyway. This is because all their constructors are private, so a subclass could not call the super constructor.;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean hasSubclassWithPublicConstructor = node.getParent()
                    .descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(n -> n.getExtendsList().stream().anyMatch(t -> t.getType().equals(node.getType())))
                    .anyMatch(n -> n.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class).anyMatch(c -> !c.isPrivate()));
                if (!hasSubclassWithPublicConstructor) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean hasSubclassInSameCompilationUnit = node.descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration::isNested)
                    .anyMatch(nested -> nested.getExtendsList().stream()
                        .anyMatch(extend -> extend.getType() != null && extend.getType().getSymbol().equals(node.getSymbol())));
                if (!hasSubclassInSameCompilationUnit) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean hasSubclass = node.getParent()
                    .descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration::isNested)
                    .anyMatch(nested -> nested.getSuperClassTypeNode() != null && nested.getSuperClassTypeNode().getType().getSymbol().equals(node.getSymbol()));
                if (!hasSubclass) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);

                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean hasSubclassInSameCompilationUnit = node.descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration::isNested)
                    .anyMatch(nestedClass -> nestedClass.getExtendsType() != null && nestedClass.getExtendsType().isReferenceToClassSameCompilationUnit());
                if (!hasSubclassInSameCompilationUnit) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean hasSubclass = node.getRoot().descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration::isNested)
                    .filter(n -> n.getSuperClassTypeNode() != null)
                    .anyMatch(n -> n.getSuperClassTypeNode().getType().getSymbol().equals(node.getSymbol()));
                if (!hasSubclass) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean hasSubclassInSameCompilationUnit = node.getRoot()
                    .descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(n -> n != node && n.getSuperClassTypeNode() != null)
                    .anyMatch(n -> n.getSuperClassTypeNode().isReferenceToClassSameCompilationUnit() && n.getSuperClassTypeNode().getSimpleName().equals(node.getSimpleName()));
                if (!hasSubclassInSameCompilationUnit) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Reports classes that may be made final because they cannot be extended from outside their compilation unit anyway. This is because all their constructors are private, so a subclass could not call the super constructor.;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean isExtended = node.getRoot().descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration::hasExtendsList)
                    .anyMatch(extendingClass -> extendingClass.getExtendsList().stream()
                        .anyMatch(extendedType -> extendedType.getType().getSymbol().equals(node.getSymbol())));
                if (!isExtended) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean hasSubclass = node.getRoot().descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(n -> n != node && n.getSuperClassTypeNode() != null && n.getSuperClassTypeNode().getType().equals(node.getType()))
                    .nonEmpty();
                if (!hasSubclass) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean hasSubclass = node.getRoot().descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration::isClass)
                    .anyMatch(subClass -> subClass.getExtendsList().stream()
                        .anyMatch(type -> type.getType().getSimpleName().equals(node.getSimpleName())));
                if (!hasSubclass) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean isExtendedWithinCompilationUnit = node.descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(n -> n.getSuperClassTypeNode() != null)
                    .anyMatch(n -> n.getSuperClassTypeNode().isReferenceToClassSameCompilationUnit());
                if (!isExtendedWithinCompilationUnit) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean isExtendedInSameCompilationUnit = node.descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration::isNested)
                    .anyMatch(nestedClass -> nestedClass.getSuperClassTypeNode() != null && nestedClass.getSuperClassTypeNode().isReferenceToClassSameCompilationUnit());
                if (!isExtendedInSameCompilationUnit) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
```

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.isNested() && node.isPrivate()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean hasSubclassInSameCompilationUnit = node.getParents()
                    .filter(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .anyMatch(parent -> parent.getSuperClassTypeNode() != null && parent.getSuperClassTypeNode().isReferenceToClassSameCompilationUnit());
                if (!hasSubclassInSameCompilationUnit) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean hasSubclassInSameCompilationUnit = node.descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration::isNested)
                    .filter(subClass -> subClass.getSuperClassTypeNode() != null)
                    .anyMatch(subClass -> subClass.getSuperClassTypeNode().isReferenceToClassSameCompilationUnit());
                if (!hasSubclassInSameCompilationUnit) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean hasSubclassInSameCompilationUnit = node.getEnclosingType()
                    .descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration::isNested)
                    .filter(n -> n.getSuperClassTypeNode() != null)
                    .anyMatch(n -> n.getSuperClassTypeNode().isReferenceToClassSameCompilationUnit() && n.getSuperClassTypeNode().getType().getSymbol().equals(node.getSymbol()));
                if (!hasSubclassInSameCompilationUnit) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean hasSubclassInSameCompilationUnit = node.descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration::isNested)
                    .filter(subClass -> subClass.getSuperClassTypeNode() != null)
                    .anyMatch(subClass -> subClass.getSuperClassTypeNode().isReferenceToClassSameCompilationUnit());
                if (!hasSubclassInSameCompilationUnit) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        } else if (node.isNested() && !node.isFinal() && node.isPrivate()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                boolean isExtended = node.getParent()
                    .descendants(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class)
                    .filter(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration::isNested)
                    .filter(n -> n.getSuperClassTypeNode() != null)
                    .anyMatch(n -> n.getSuperClassTypeNode().isReferenceToClassSameCompilationUnit() && n.getSuperClassTypeNode().getSimpleName().equals(node.getSimpleName()));
                if (!isExtended) {
                    addViolation(data, node);
                }
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;

public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
```
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic() && !node.isAbstract()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override

        return super.visit(node, data);

```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
```
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic() && !node.isAbstract()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

```
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;

    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);

    @Override

        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic() && !node.isAbstract() && !node.isNested()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
```
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic() && !node.isAbstract()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);

You are an expert in writing java rule checkers in PMD tool version 7.0.0. 
You have helped me write a checker for this rule:
Rule description: Reports classes that may be made final because they cannot be extended from outside their compilation unit anyway. This is because all their constructors are private, so a subclass could not call the super constructor.;
And the source code of the checker is as follows:
```
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;

import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}
```

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic() && !node.isAbstract()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate && !node.isAbstract() && !node.isPrivate()) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }
}

```java
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.*;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public boolean hasAnnotations(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node){
    NodeStream<ASTAnnotation> annotations = node.getDeclaredAnnotations();
    return annotations.nonEmpty();
}
```

================修复新加测试用例后生成的checker===================
package net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.design;

import java.util.*;
import java.lang.*;


import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.rule.AbstractJavaRulechainRule;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.ast.internal. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.types. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.java.symbols. *;
import net.sourceforge.pmd.lang.ast.NodeStream;
public class ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule extends AbstractJavaRulechainRule {
    public ClassWithOnlyPrivateConstructorsShouldBeFinalRule() {
        super(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration.class, ASTConstructorDeclaration.class);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node, Object data) {
        if (!node.isFinal() && node.isPublic()) {
            boolean allConstructorsPrivate = node.descendants(ASTConstructorDeclaration.class)
                .all(ASTConstructorDeclaration::isPrivate);
            if (allConstructorsPrivate && !hasLombokValueAnnotation(node)) {
                addViolation(data, node);
            }
        }
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    @Override
    public Object visit(ASTConstructorDeclaration node, Object data) {
        return super.visit(node, data);
    }

    private boolean hasLombokValueAnnotation(ASTClassOrInterfaceDeclaration node) {
        return node.getDeclaredAnnotations()
            .any(annotation -> "Value".equals(annotation.getAnnotationName()));
    }
}
